# non-free-opportunities >> opportunity-paid (OpenBookingApprovalFlow >> Multiple)

**Booking Flow:** OpenBookingApprovalFlow

**Opportunity Type:** Multiple

**Feature:** Payment / Opportunities with a non-zero price (Implemented) 

**Test:**  Successful booking with payment property

A successful end to end booking of a non-free opportunity with the `payment` property included if required.

### Running only this test

```bash
npm start -- --runInBand test/features/payment/non-free-opportunities/implemented/opportunity-paid-test.js
```
